USERMESSAGE #7
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Template System Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides template selection and management for document rendering.
     5→ * PoC Implementation: Uses code-level template switching via ACTIVE_TEMPLATE constant.
     6→ * (See DECISIONS.md Decision 4: UI dropdown is post-PoC feature)
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    10→import CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'
    11→import CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'
    12→import CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'
    13→
    14→// Template metadata interface for future extensibility
    15→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    16→  name: string
    17→  displayName: string
    18→  description: string
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Template registry type
    22→export interface TemplateRegistry {
    23→  [key: string]: {
    24→    component: Component
    25→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    26→  }
    27→}
    28→
    29→/**
    30→ * ACTIVE_TEMPLATE Constant
    31→ *
    32→ * Change this constant to switch templates in the PoC.
    33→ * Available options: 'modern', 'classic', 'minimal'
    34→ *
    35→ * Example:
    36→ *   const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'modern'  // Uses Modern template (default)
    37→ *   const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'classic' // Uses Classic template (table-based layout)
    38→ *   const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'minimal' // Uses Minimal template (clean, minimalist style)
    39→ *
    40→ * Template Descriptions:
    41→ * - modern: Professional cover letter with modern styling, semantic HTML (article/header)
    42→ * - classic: Traditional cover letter with table-based layout, uppercase headers
    43→ * - minimal: Clean, minimalist design with simple div structure and generous whitespace
    44→ */
    45→const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'modern'
    46→
    47→/**
    48→ * Template Registry
    49→ *
    50→ * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.
    51→ * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.
    52→ */
    53→const templates: TemplateRegistry = {
    54→  modern: {
    55→    component: CoverLetterModern,
    56→    metadata: {
    57→      name: 'modern',
    58→      displayName: 'Modern',
    59→      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',
    60→    },
    61→  },
    62→  classic: {
    63→    component: CoverLetterClassic,
    64→    metadata: {
    65→      name: 'classic',
    66→      displayName: 'Classic',
    67→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    68→    },
    69→  },
    70→  minimal: {
    71→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    72→    metadata: {
    73→      name: 'minimal',
    74→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    75→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    76→    },
    77→  },
    78→}
    79→
    80→/**
    81→ * Get the currently active template component
    82→ *
    83→ * @returns The Vue component for the active template
    84→ * @throws Error if the active template is not found in the registry
    85→ */
    86→export function getCurrentTemplate(): Component {
    87→  const templateEntry = templates[ACTIVE_TEMPLATE]
    88→
    89→  if (!templateEntry) {
    90→    throw new Error(
    91→      `Template "${ACTIVE_TEMPLATE}" not found. Available templates: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`
    92→    )
    93→  }
    94→
    95→  return templateEntry.component
    96→}
    97→
    98→/**
    99→ * Get metadata for the currently active template
   100→ *
   101→ * @returns Template metadata for the active template
   102→ */
   103→export function getCurrentTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata {
   104→  const templateEntry = templates[ACTIVE_TEMPLATE]
   105→
   106→  if (!templateEntry) {
   107→    throw new Error(
   108→      `Template "${ACTIVE_TEMPLATE}" not found. Available templates: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`
   109→    )
   110→  }
   111→
   112→  return templateEntry.metadata
   113→}
   114→
   115→/**
   116→ * Get all available template names
   117→ *
   118→ * @returns Array of template names
   119→ */
   120→export function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   121→  return Object.keys(templates)
   122→}
   123→
   124→/**
   125→ * Get metadata for all available templates
   126→ *
   127→ * @returns Array of template metadata objects
   128→ */
   129→export function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   130→  return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   131→}
   132→
   133→/**
   134→ * Composable function to use template system in Vue components
   135→ *
   136→ * @returns Object with template selection functions
   137→ */
   138→export function useTemplate() {
   139→  return {
   140→    getCurrentTemplate,
   141→    getCurrentTemplateMetadata,
   142→    getAvailableTemplates,
   143→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   144→    activeTemplate: ACTIVE_TEMPLATE,
   145→  }
   146→}
   147→

    23→            <line x1="16" y1="13" x2="8" y2="13" />

    26→          </svg>
    27→        </div>
    28→        <h2 class="welcome-headline">
    29→          Create professional documents in seconds
    30→        </h2>
    31→        <p class="welcome-description">
    32→          Write structured XML, pick a template, and instantly preview a polished document — ready to export.
    33→        </p>
    34→        <UButton
    35→          size="xl"
    36→          color="primary"

    39→          @click="loadSample"
    40→        >
    41→          Start with a sample

    44→    </div>
    45→

    48→      <!-- Left Panel: XML Editor -->
    49→      <div class="editor-panel">
    50→        <XmlEditor
    51→          v-model="xmlContent"
    52→          height="100%"
    53→          width="100%"
    54→        />
    55→      </div>
    56→
    57→      <!-- Right Panel: Preview -->
    58→      <div class="preview-panel">
    59→        <PreviewPanel
    60→          :xml-content="debouncedXmlContent"
    61→          :zoom="1"
    62→        />
    63→      </div>
    64→    </div>
    65→  </div>
    66→</template>
    67→
    68→<script setup lang="ts">
    69→import { ref, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Main Application Page - MVP 6: Dual-Panel Integration
    73→ *
    74→ * Features:
    75→ * - Welcome screen on first load (no saved data in localStorage)
    76→ * - Dual-panel 50/50 layout (CSS Grid)
    77→ * - 300ms debounced real-time updates (per DECISIONS.md)
    78→ * - Persists XML content to localStorage
    79→ * - Minimum 1024px responsive design
    80→ */
    81→
    82→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_xml_content'
    83→
    84→// Set page metadata
    85→useHead({
    86→  title: 'OhMyDoc - XML to HTML Transformer',
    87→})
    88→
    89→// Welcome screen is shown when no saved data exists
    90→const showWelcome = ref(true)
    91→const isSampleLoading = ref(false)
    92→
    93→// Reactive state for XML content
    94→const xmlContent = ref('')
    95→const debouncedXmlContent = ref('')
    96→
    97→// Debounce timer ref
    98→let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
    99→
   100→/**
   101→ * Debounce watcher: Updates preview 300ms after user stops typing
   102→ * Per DECISIONS.md Decision 5: 300ms < 500ms threshold provides smooth UX
   103→ * without feeling laggy or causing excessive re-parsing
   104→ */
   105→watch(xmlContent, (newValue) => {
   106→  if (debounceTimer) {
   107→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   108→  }
   109→
   110→  debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   111→    debouncedXmlContent.value = newValue
   112→    // Persist to localStorage so returning users skip the welcome screen
   113→    try {
   114→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, newValue)
   115→    }
   116→    catch {
   117→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   118→    }
   119→  }, 300)
   120→})
   121→
   122→/**
   123→ * Fetch and apply the sample cover letter XML.
   124→ * Called by the "Start with a sample" button on the welcome screen.
   125→ */
   126→async function loadSample() {
   127→  isSampleLoading.value = true
   128→  try {
   129→    const response = await fetch('/samples/cover-letter.xml')
   130→    if (!response.ok) {
   131→      throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`)
   132→    }
   133→    const sampleXml = await response.text()
   134→    xmlContent.value = sampleXml
   135→    debouncedXmlContent.value = sampleXml
   136→    showWelcome.value = false
   137→  }
   138→  catch (error) {
   139→    console.error('Error loading sample XML:', error)
   140→    // Still dismiss welcome and show an empty editor rather than getting stuck
   141→    showWelcome.value = false
   142→  }
   143→  finally {
   144→    isSampleLoading.value = false
   145→  }
   146→}
   147→
   148→/**
   149→ * On mount: restore saved content from localStorage.
   150→ * If content exists, skip the welcome screen and load it directly.
   151→ */
   152→onMounted(() => {
   153→  try {
   154→    const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
   155→    if (saved) {
   156→      xmlContent.value = saved
   157→      debouncedXmlContent.value = saved
   158→      showWelcome.value = false
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→  catch {
   162→    // Ignore localStorage errors; welcome screen will show as default
   163→  }
   164→})
   165→
   166→/**
   167→ * Cleanup: Clear debounce timer on component unmount
   168→ */
   169→onUnmounted(() => {
   170→  if (debounceTimer) {
   171→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   172→  }
   173→})
   174→</script>
   175→
   176→<style scoped>
   177→/**
   178→ * Main app container - full viewport height
   179→ */
   180→.app-container {

   182→  flex-direction: column;
   183→  height: 100vh;
   184→  width: 100vw;
   185→  overflow: hidden;

   188→/**

   193→.dual-panel-layout {
   194→  display: grid;
   195→  grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr;

   198→  gap: 0;

   201→  min-width: 1024px;

   208→.editor-panel {

   214→}

   224→  background-color: var(--color-gray-50);
   225→}
   226→
   227→/**
   228→ * Responsive design for smaller screens

   231→@media (max-width: 1024px) {
   232→  .dual-panel-layout {
   233→    grid-template-columns: 1fr;
   234→    grid-template-rows: 1fr 1fr;
   235→    min-width: unset;
   236→  }
   237→

    40→import type { ParsedData } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'

    42→// Ensure this component only runs on the client side (DOMParser is browser-only)
    43→defineOptions({
    44→  name: 'PreviewPanel',
    45→})
    46→
    47→/**
    48→ * PreviewPanel Component
    49→ *
    50→ * Integration point combining XML parser (MVP 2) and template system (MVP 3).
    51→ * Provides real-time preview of XML content with error handling and zoom support.
    52→ *
    53→ * Props:
    54→ * - xmlContent: XML string to parse and render
    55→ * - zoom: Zoom level for scaling (default: 1, range: 0.75 - 1.5)
    56→ */
    57→
    58→interface Props {
    59→  xmlContent: string
    60→  zoom?: number
    61→}
    62→
    63→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
    64→  zoom: 1,
    65→})
    66→
    67→// Reactive state
    68→const parsedData = ref<ParsedData | undefined>(undefined)
    69→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    70→const isLoading = ref(false)
    71→const templateComponent = ref<Component | undefined>(undefined)
    72→
    73→// Get composables
    74→const { parseXml } = useXmlParser()
    75→
    76→// Computed style for zoom transform
    77→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    78→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    79→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    80→}))
    81→
    82→/**
    83→ * Parse XML and update component state
    84→ * Handles all parsing errors gracefully with user-friendly messages
    85→ */
    86→function updatePreview() {
    87→  // Reset state
    88→  isLoading.value = true
    89→  error.value = undefined
    90→  parsedData.value = undefined
    91→  templateComponent.value = undefined
    92→
    93→  try {
    94→    // Get the current template component
    95→    templateComponent.value = getCurrentTemplate()
    96→
    97→    // Parse XML content
    98→    const result = parseXml(props.xmlContent)
    99→
   100→    if (result.success && result.data) {
   101→      // Success: update parsed data
   102→      parsedData.value = result.data
   103→      error.value = undefined
   104→    }
   105→    else {
   106→      // Parsing failed: show user-friendly error
   107→      error.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
   108→      parsedData.value = undefined
   109→    }
   110→  }
   111→  catch (err) {
   112→    // Catch any unexpected errors (e.g., template not found)
   113→    const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
   114→    error.value = `Preview error: ${errorMessage}`
   115→    parsedData.value = undefined
   116→  }
   117→  finally {
   118→    isLoading.value = false
   119→  }
   120→}
   121→
   122→// Watch for changes to xmlContent and re-parse automatically
   123→watch(
   124→  () => props.xmlContent,
   125→  () => {
   126→    updatePreview()
   127→  },
   128→  { immediate: true },
   129→)
   130→</script>
   131→
   132→<style scoped>
   133→.preview-panel {
   134→  width: 100%;
   135→  height: 100%;
   136→  overflow: auto;
   137→  background-color: var(--color-gray-50);
   138→  padding: 1rem;
   139→}
   140→
   141→.error-alert {
   142→  margin-bottom: 1rem;
   143→}
   144→
   145→.loading-state,
   146→.placeholder-state {
   147→  display: flex;
   148→  align-items: center;
   149→  justify-content: center;
   150→  min-height: 200px;
   151→  color: var(--color-gray-600);
   152→}
   153→
   154→.preview-container {
   155→  width: fit-content;
   156→  min-width: 100%;
   157→  /* Ensure zoom transform doesn't clip content */
   158→  padding-bottom: 2rem;
   159→}

    16→import type { editor } from 'monaco-editor'
    17→
    18→// Props definition for v-model support and customization
    19→interface Props {
    20→  modelValue: string
    21→  height?: string
    22→  width?: string
    23→  readonly?: boolean
    24→}
    25→
    26→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
    27→  height: '100%',
    28→  width: '100%',
    29→  readonly: false
    30→})
    31→
    32→// Emits for v-model two-way binding and error handling
    33→const emit = defineEmits<{
    34→  'update:modelValue': [value: string]
    35→  'error': [error: string]
    36→}>()
    37→
    38→// Editor state
    39→const editorContent = ref(props.modelValue)
    40→const editorInstance = ref<editor.IStandaloneCodeEditor | null>(null)
    41→const language = ref('xml')
    42→
    43→// Monaco Editor configuration
    44→const editorOptions = computed(() => ({
    45→  // Basic editor features
    46→  automaticLayout: true,
    47→  lineNumbers: 'on' as const,
    48→  readOnly: props.readonly,
    49→
    50→  // XML-specific formatting
    51→  tabSize: 2,
    52→  insertSpaces: true,
    53→  autoIndent: 'full' as const,
    54→
    55→  // Editor behavior
    56→  wordWrap: 'on' as const,
    57→  minimap: {
    58→    enabled: true,
    59→    maxColumn: 120
    60→  },
    61→
    62→  // XML language features
    63→  folding: true,
    64→  foldingStrategy: 'indentation' as const,
    65→  bracketPairColorization: {
    66→    enabled: true
    67→  },
    68→
    69→  // Scrolling and rendering
    70→  scrollBeyondLastLine: false,
    71→  renderWhitespace: 'selection' as const,
    72→
    73→  // Font and display
    74→  fontSize: 14,
    75→  fontFamily: 'Consolas, "Courier New", monospace',
    76→  lineHeight: 21,
    77→
    78→  // Accessibility
    79→  accessibilitySupport: 'auto' as const,
    80→
    81→  // Suggest and IntelliSense
    82→  quickSuggestions: {
    83→    other: true,
    84→    comments: false,
    85→    strings: true
    86→  },
    87→  suggestOnTriggerCharacters: true,
    88→  acceptSuggestionOnEnter: 'on' as const,
    89→
    90→  // Auto-closing
    91→  autoClosingBrackets: 'languageDefined' as const,
    92→  autoClosingQuotes: 'languageDefined' as const,
    93→  autoSurround: 'languageDefined' as const
    94→}))
    95→
    96→// Watch for prop changes and update editor content
    97→watch(() => props.modelValue, (newValue) => {
    98→  if (newValue !== editorContent.value) {
    99→    editorContent.value = newValue
   100→  }
   101→})
   102→
   103→// Watch for editor content changes and emit to parent
   104→watch(editorContent, (newValue) => {
   105→  emit('update:modelValue', newValue)
   106→})
   107→
   108→// Handle editor mount event
   109→const handleEditorMount = (editor: editor.IStandaloneCodeEditor) => {
   110→  editorInstance.value = editor
   111→
   112→  // Ensure XML language is set
   113→  const model = editor.getModel()
   114→  if (model) {
   115→    // Monaco automatically handles XML syntax highlighting
   116→    // when language is set to 'xml'
   117→  }
   118→}
   119→
   120→// Cleanup on component unmount
   121→onBeforeUnmount(() => {
   122→  if (editorInstance.value) {
   123→    editorInstance.value.dispose()
   124→    editorInstance.value = null
   125→  }
   126→})
   127→
   128→// Expose editor instance for advanced usage if needed
   129→defineExpose({
   130→  getEditor: () => editorInstance.value
   131→})
   132→</script>
   133→
   134→<style scoped>
   135→.xml-editor-wrapper {
   136→  position: relative;
   137→  overflow: hidden;
   138→}

## File Contents Summary

### 1. **composables/useTemplate.ts**
This composable provides template management with:

- **Templates registry**: Defines three templates (modern, classic, minimal) with components and metadata
- **Functions**:
  - `getCurrentTemplate()`: Returns the active template component
  - `getCurrentTemplateMetadata()`: Returns active template metadata
  - `getAvailableTemplates()`: Returns array of template names
  - `getAllTemplateMetadata()`: Returns all template metadata

Simple header component using `@nuxt/ui`:
- Contains `<UContainer>` wrapper
- Three-section layout (left actions, center title, right actions)
- Title: "OhMyDoc v2" with tagline "XML to HTML Transformer"
- Has named slots for future action buttons:
  - `left-actions`: For Format, Clear, Import buttons (MVP 8)
  - `right-actions`: For Export and Zoom buttons (MVPs 7 & 9)

### 3. **pages/index.vue**

- **AppHeader component** with empty action slots
- **Welcome screen** (shown on first load when no localStorage data):
  - Icon, headline, description
  - "Start with a sample" button using `<UButton>`
- **Dual-panel layout** (when not showing welcome):
  - Left panel: XmlEditor (100% height)
  - Right panel: PreviewPanel (scrollable)
- **State management**:
  - `xmlContent`: Reactive XML content
  - `debouncedXmlContent`: 300ms debounced version
  - `showWelcome`: Toggle welcome screen
  - localStorage persistence with key `'ohmydoc_xml_content'`

### 4. **components/PreviewPanel.vue**

- **Props**: `xmlContent` (string) and `zoom` (number, default: 1)
- **Uses composables**: `useXmlParser()` and `getCurrentTemplate()`
- **States**:
  - Error: Shows `<UAlert>` with parsing error
  - Loading: Shows "Parsing XML..."
  - Success: Renders template component with parsed data
  - Placeholder: Shows when no valid XML
- **Features**:
  - Zoom support via `transform: scale()`
  - Graceful error handling with user-friendly messages

## Key Technical Details

**Debouncing Strategy**: 300ms debounce between XML input and preview (per DECISIONS.md)

**Component Architecture**:
- Components use v-model for two-way binding
- Composables for shared logic (no Pinia/Vuex)
- Named slots for extensibility

**@nuxt/ui Integration**:
- Used for application UI (buttons, cards, alerts, inputs)
- NOT used in document templates (only scoped CSS for exportability)
- Supports dark mode via CSS utilities

**Editor**: Uses `nuxt-monaco-editor` with XML language support and advanced formatting

This project is well-structured for MVP development with clear separation between UI components and template-based rendering!

     1→/**
     2→ * Template System Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides template selection and management for document rendering.
     5→ * PoC Implementation: Uses code-level template switching via ACTIVE_TEMPLATE constant.
     6→ * (See DECISIONS.md Decision 4: UI dropdown is post-PoC feature)
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    10→import CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'
    11→import CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'
    12→import CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'
    13→
    14→// Template metadata interface for future extensibility
    15→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    16→  name: string
    17→  displayName: string
    18→  description: string
    19→}
    20→
    21→// Template registry type
    22→export interface TemplateRegistry {
    23→  [key: string]: {
    24→    component: Component
    25→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    26→  }
    27→}
    28→
    29→/**
    30→ * ACTIVE_TEMPLATE Constant
    31→ *
    32→ * Change this constant to switch templates in the PoC.
    33→ * Available options: 'modern', 'classic', 'minimal'
    34→ *
    35→ * Example:
    36→ *   const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'modern'  // Uses Modern template (default)
    37→ *   const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'classic' // Uses Classic template (table-based layout)
    38→ *   const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'minimal' // Uses Minimal template (clean, minimalist style)
    39→ *
    40→ * Template Descriptions:
    41→ * - modern: Professional cover letter with modern styling, semantic HTML (article/header)
    42→ * - classic: Traditional cover letter with table-based layout, uppercase headers
    43→ * - minimal: Clean, minimalist design with simple div structure and generous whitespace
    44→ */
    45→const ACTIVE_TEMPLATE = 'modern'
    46→
    47→/**
    48→ * Template Registry
    49→ *
    50→ * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.
    51→ * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.
    52→ */
    53→const templates: TemplateRegistry = {
    54→  modern: {
    55→    component: CoverLetterModern,
    56→    metadata: {
    57→      name: 'modern',
    58→      displayName: 'Modern',
    59→      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',
    60→    },
    61→  },
    62→  classic: {
    63→    component: CoverLetterClassic,
    64→    metadata: {
    65→      name: 'classic',
    66→      displayName: 'Classic',
    67→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    68→    },
    69→  },
    70→  minimal: {
    71→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    72→    metadata: {
    73→      name: 'minimal',
    74→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    75→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    76→    },
    77→  },
    78→}
    79→
    80→/**
    81→ * Get the currently active template component
    82→ *
    83→ * @returns The Vue component for the active template
    84→ * @throws Error if the active template is not found in the registry
    85→ */
    86→export function getCurrentTemplate(): Component {
    87→  const templateEntry = templates[ACTIVE_TEMPLATE]
    88→
    89→  if (!templateEntry) {
    90→    throw new Error(
    91→      `Template "${ACTIVE_TEMPLATE}" not found. Available templates: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`
    92→    )
    93→  }
    94→
    95→  return templateEntry.component
    96→}
    97→
    98→/**
    99→ * Get metadata for the currently active template
   100→ *
   101→ * @returns Template metadata for the active template
   102→ */
   103→export function getCurrentTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata {
   104→  const templateEntry = templates[ACTIVE_TEMPLATE]
   105→
   106→  if (!templateEntry) {
   107→    throw new Error(
   108→      `Template "${ACTIVE_TEMPLATE}" not found. Available templates: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`
   109→    )
   110→  }
   111→
   112→  return templateEntry.metadata
   113→}
   114→
   115→/**
   116→ * Get all available template names
   117→ *
   118→ * @returns Array of template names
   119→ */
   120→export function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   121→  return Object.keys(templates)
   122→}
   123→
   124→/**
   125→ * Get metadata for all available templates
   126→ *
   127→ * @returns Array of template metadata objects
   128→ */
   129→export function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   130→  return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   131→}
   132→
   133→/**
   134→ * Composable function to use template system in Vue components
   135→ *
   136→ * @returns Object with template selection functions
   137→ */
   138→export function useTemplate() {
   139→  return {
   140→    getCurrentTemplate,
   141→    getCurrentTemplateMetadata,
   142→    getAvailableTemplates,
   143→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   144→    activeTemplate: ACTIVE_TEMPLATE,
   145→  }
   146→}

    68→<script setup lang="ts">
    69→import { ref, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Main Application Page - MVP 6: Dual-Panel Integration
    73→ *
    74→ * Features:
    75→ * - Welcome screen on first load (no saved data in localStorage)
    76→ * - Dual-panel 50/50 layout (CSS Grid)
    77→ * - 300ms debounced real-time updates (per DECISIONS.md)
    78→ * - Persists XML content to localStorage
    79→ * - Minimum 1024px responsive design
    80→ */
    81→
    82→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_xml_content'
    83→
    84→// Set page metadata
    85→useHead({
    86→  title: 'OhMyDoc - XML to HTML Transformer',
    87→})
    88→
    89→// Welcome screen is shown when no saved data exists
    90→const showWelcome = ref(true)
    91→const isSampleLoading = ref(false)
    92→
    93→// Reactive state for XML content
    94→const xmlContent = ref('')
    95→const debouncedXmlContent = ref('')
    96→
    97→// Debounce timer ref
    98→let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
    99→
   100→/**
   101→ * Debounce watcher: Updates preview 300ms after user stops typing
   102→ * Per DECISIONS.md Decision 5: 300ms < 500ms threshold provides smooth UX
   103→ * without feeling laggy or causing excessive re-parsing
   104→ */
   105→watch(xmlContent, (newValue) => {
   106→  if (debounceTimer) {
   107→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   108→  }
   109→
   110→  debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   111→    debouncedXmlContent.value = newValue
   112→    // Persist to localStorage so returning users skip the welcome screen
   113→    try {
   114→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, newValue)
   115→    }
   116→    catch {
   117→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   118→    }
   119→  }, 300)
   120→})
   121→
   122→/**
   123→ * Fetch and apply the sample cover letter XML.
   124→ * Called by the "Start with a sample" button on the welcome screen.
   125→ */
   126→async function loadSample() {
   127→  isSampleLoading.value = true
   128→  try {
   129→    const response = await fetch('/samples/cover-letter.xml')
   130→    if (!response.ok) {
   131→      throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`)
   132→    }
   133→    const sampleXml = await response.text()
   134→    xmlContent.value = sampleXml
   135→    debouncedXmlContent.value = sampleXml
   136→    showWelcome.value = false
   137→  }
   138→  catch (error) {
   139→    console.error('Error loading sample XML:', error)
   140→    // Still dismiss welcome and show an empty editor rather than getting stuck
   141→    showWelcome.value = false
   142→  }
   143→  finally {
   144→    isSampleLoading.value = false
   145→  }
   146→}
   147→
   148→/**
   149→ * On mount: restore saved content from localStorage.
   150→ * If content exists, skip the welcome screen and load it directly.
   151→ */
   152→onMounted(() => {
   153→  try {
   154→    const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
   155→    if (saved) {
   156→      xmlContent.value = saved
   157→      debouncedXmlContent.value = saved
   158→      showWelcome.value = false
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→  catch {
   162→    // Ignore localStorage errors; welcome screen will show as default
   163→  }
   164→})
   165→
   166→/**
   167→ * Cleanup: Clear debounce timer on component unmount
   168→ */
   169→onUnmounted(() => {
   170→  if (debounceTimer) {
   171→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   172→  }
   173→})

    35→<script setup lang="ts">
    36→import { ref, computed, watch } from 'vue'
    37→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    38→import { useXmlParser } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
    39→import { getCurrentTemplate } from '~/composables/useTemplate'

    41→
    42→// Ensure this component only runs on the client side (DOMParser is browser-only)
    43→defineOptions({
    44→  name: 'PreviewPanel',
    45→})
    46→
    47→/**
    48→ * PreviewPanel Component
    49→ *
    50→ * Integration point combining XML parser (MVP 2) and template system (MVP 3).
    51→ * Provides real-time preview of XML content with error handling and zoom support.
    52→ *
    53→ * Props:
    54→ * - xmlContent: XML string to parse and render
    55→ * - zoom: Zoom level for scaling (default: 1, range: 0.75 - 1.5)
    56→ */
    57→
    58→interface Props {
    59→  xmlContent: string
    60→  zoom?: number
    61→}
    62→
    63→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
    64→  zoom: 1,
    65→})
    66→
    67→// Reactive state
    68→const parsedData = ref<ParsedData | undefined>(undefined)
    69→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    70→const isLoading = ref(false)
    71→const templateComponent = ref<Component | undefined>(undefined)
    72→
    73→// Get composables
    74→const { parseXml } = useXmlParser()
    75→
    76→// Computed style for zoom transform
    77→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    78→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    79→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    80→}))
    81→
    82→/**
    83→ * Parse XML and update component state
    84→ * Handles all parsing errors gracefully with user-friendly messages
    85→ */
    86→function updatePreview() {
    87→  // Reset state
    88→  isLoading.value = true
    89→  error.value = undefined
    90→  parsedData.value = undefined
    91→  templateComponent.value = undefined
    92→
    93→  try {
    94→    // Get the current template component
    95→    templateComponent.value = getCurrentTemplate()
    96→
    97→    // Parse XML content
    98→    const result = parseXml(props.xmlContent)
    99→
   100→    if (result.success && result.data) {
   101→      // Success: update parsed data
   102→      parsedData.value = result.data
   103→      error.value = undefined
   104→    }
   105→    else {
   106→      // Parsing failed: show user-friendly error
   107→      error.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
   108→      parsedData.value = undefined
   109→    }
   110→  }
   111→  catch (err) {
   112→    // Catch any unexpected errors (e.g., template not found)
   113→    const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
   114→    error.value = `Preview error: ${errorMessage}`
   115→    parsedData.value = undefined
   116→  }
   117→  finally {
   118→    isLoading.value = false
   119→  }
   120→}
   121→
   122→// Watch for changes to xmlContent and re-parse automatically
   123→watch(
   124→  () => props.xmlContent,
   125→  () => {
   126→    updatePreview()
   127→  },
   128→  { immediate: true },
   129→)

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #37
Now I have a clear picture of the codebase. Here's my plan: 1. **Modify `composables/useTemplate.ts`**: Convert the static `ACTIVE_TEMPLATE` constant to a reactive ref, add localStorage persistence, and expose a `setActiveTemplate` function. The composable needs to use `useState` (Nuxt's composable for shared state) or a simple `ref` - but since the template state needs to be shared between AppHeader and PreviewPanel, I should use `useState` from Nuxt or simply export a shared ref. Actually, looking at the architecture: - The composable currently returns static functions - I need to make the active template reactive and shared - The cleanest approach would be to use a module-level `ref` (shared state) in the composable 2. **Modify `components/AppHeader.vue`**: Add a `USelect` or `USelectMenu` dropdown that lists available templates and emits/updates the selected template. 3. **Modify `components/PreviewPanel.vue`**: Make it reactive to template changes (watch the active template, not just xmlContent). 4. **Modify `pages/index.vue`**: Pass the selected template to PreviewPanel, or connect the template switcher. The key is ensuring the template state flows properly through the component hierarchy so that switching templates in the header immediately updates the preview. For the composable, I'll use a module-level reactive ref to store the active template with localStorage persistence, and export a setter function so components can update it. Since this is a client-side app, the shared ref approach will work fine—I could also use Nuxt's `useState` for the same effect, but a simple ref is more straightforward here. I need to refactor the template system to be properly reactive across components. I'll create a `useTemplate` composable that manages the active template state with localStorage persistence, then update the header to include a template switcher dropdown and make the preview panel watch for template changes so it re-renders when the user selects a different template. Building the composable... I'm setting up a hook that manages the active template state, checking localStorage on the client side to persist the user's choice and defaulting to 'modern'. The setActiveTemplate function validates the template exists before updating it and safely saves to localStorage, while getCurrentTemplate retrieves the actual component for the currently selected template. Now I'm adding helper functions to expose template metadata and list all available templates, then returning everything as a composable. I'm also creating a backward-compatible export for direct access to getCurrentTemplate that handles the template lookup independently. But I'm realizing there's a reactivity issue here—the standalone getCurrentTemplate function reads from localStorage but doesn't update when the user switches templates through the composable, so I need to rethink this approach. The solution is to use a reactive state in the composable and have PreviewPanel watch that activeTemplate value instead of calling a static function. I'll refactor PreviewPanel to use the composable and set up a watcher that triggers updates whenever either the XML content or the active template changes. I need to be careful about backward compatibility—the `PreviewPanel.vue` currently imports `getCurrentTemplate` as a standalone function, so I should update that to use the composable instead. For `PreviewPanel.vue`, I'll switch to importing `useTemplate` and create a computed property for `templateComponent` that reacts to changes in `activeTemplate`, while also watching both `xmlContent` and `activeTemplate` to trigger re-renders. In `AppHeader.vue`, I'll add a template selector dropdown using `USelect` that integrates with the `useTemplate` composable to manage the active template selection. Now I'm ready to implement these changes, starting with the `AppHeader.vue` component where I need to figure out where to place the template selector in the existing layout structure. I'm realizing there's a potential hydration mismatch if the server initializes the state differently than what's stored in localStorage, so for a pure client-side app, I should initialize `useState` with a default value and then use `onMounted` to sync with localStorage to avoid any SSR conflicts. Since composables can't directly use lifecycle hooks unless called within a component, the cleanest approach is either using a module-level `ref` for simplicity, or wrapping the localStorage sync in a callback that components can call on mount. I'm settling on Nuxt's `useState` for reactivity across components, then initializing from localStorage inside an `onMounted` hook within the composable itself—this way the template preference persists and syncs properly. Setting up the composable... I'm laying out the implementation plan: update the composable to use reactive state with localStorage initialization, add template selection to AppHeader, and refactor PreviewPanel to use the composable instead of direct imports. But I'm realizing there's a timing issue with `useState` and `onMounted` that I need to work through—specifically, how to ensure localStorage loads once without duplicate initialization when multiple components use the composable. the composable return. I'm setting up the composable to expose `activeTemplate` and a `setActiveTemplate` function that handles both the reactive state update and localStorage persistence, with error handling for storage failures. Now I'm adding computed properties and helper methods to retrieve template data—getting the current component, listing available templates, and accessing metadata. I'll keep the standalone `getCurrentTemplate` export for backward compatibility with PreviewPanel, though I could refactor that component to use the composable instead. For PreviewPanel, I need to update the `templateComponent` ref to be a computed property that safely accesses the current template from the composable, but since PreviewPanel doesn't have direct access to the templates object, I should expose `currentTemplate` from the composable itself. There's a timing consideration with `onMounted` in the composable—it runs during component setup, so if both AppHeader and PreviewPanel call `useTemplate()`, localStorage gets read twice, but that's acceptable since the first read establishes the initial state. Now I need to finalize the implementation and make sure `onMounted` is properly imported in the composable file. I'll set up the AppHeader component with a select dropdown that binds to the template state, using the standard USelect format with label and value pairs for the available templates. ASSISTANTMESSAGE #55
SSR is enabled by default (no `ssr: false`). So I need to be careful about localStorage access. The safest approach for the `useState` initializer: use `import.meta.client` to only access localStorage on the client, and fall back to 'modern' on server. ```typescript const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => { if (import.meta.client) { try { const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY) if (saved && Object.keys(templates).includes(saved)) { return saved } } catch {} } return 'modern' }) ``` But wait—with SSR enabled, the server initializes `activeTemplate` to 'modern' and sends that in the hydration payload. The client won't re-run the initializer since the state already exists, so the localStorage value never gets read. I need to use `onMounted` in the composable instead to override the state after hydration completes. Setting up the composable with localStorage sync... The issue is that both `AppHeader.vue` and `PreviewPanel.vue` will call `useTemplate()`, which means each component registers its own `onMounted` hook that reads from localStorage. Since they're setting the same value, there's redundant work happening. I can use Nuxt's `callOnce` utility to ensure the localStorage initialization only runs once across the entire application, regardless of how many components use the composable. The `onMounted` hook will load the saved template after hydration, which means there might be a brief flash where the default template shows before switching to what's in localStorage. However, since PreviewPanel needs JavaScript to render anyway (it uses Monaco editor), users won't actually see this flicker, and the SSR output would just display a "No content" state initially. I'll go with the `onMounted` approach. My plan is to update the composable to use `useState` for shared state across components, initialize it from localStorage on mount, and add a setter function. For PreviewPanel, I need to decide whether to keep the standalone `getCurrentTemplate` function for backward compatibility or refactor it to use the composable directly—updating the component to use the composable seems cleaner. I need to check where these standalone functions are actually being used throughout the codebase before deciding whether to keep them or refactor them into the composable.

  "content": "/**\n * Template System Composable\n *\n * Provides reactive template selection and management for document rendering.\n * Active template is shared across all components via useState and persisted\n * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.\n */\n\nimport { onMounted, computed } from 'vue'\nimport type { Component } from 'vue'\nimport CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'\nimport CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'\nimport CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'\n\nconst LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_template'\n\n// Template metadata interface for future extensibility\nexport interface TemplateMetadata {\n  name: string\n  displayName: string\n  description: string\n}\n\n// Template registry type\nexport interface TemplateRegistry {\n  [key: string]: {\n    component: Component\n    metadata: TemplateMetadata\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * Template Registry\n *\n * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.\n * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.\n */\nconst templates: TemplateRegistry = {\n  modern: {\n    component: CoverLetterModern,\n    metadata: {\n      name: 'modern',\n      displayName: 'Modern',\n      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',\n    },\n  },\n  classic: {\n    component: CoverLetterClassic,\n    metadata: {\n      name: 'classic',\n      displayName: 'Classic',\n      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',\n    },\n  },\n  minimal: {\n    component: CoverLetterMinimal,\n    metadata: {\n      name: 'minimal',\n      displayName: 'Minimal',\n      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',\n    },\n  },\n}\n\n/**\n * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.\n *\n * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.\n * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).\n *\n * @returns Reactive template state and control functions\n */\nexport function useTemplate() {\n  // Shared reactive state \u2014 useState ensures all components see the same value\n  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')\n\n  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)\n  onMounted(() => {\n    try {\n      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)\n      if (saved && templates[saved]) {\n        activeTemplate.value = saved\n      }\n    }\n    catch {\n      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)\n    }\n  })\n\n  /**\n   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.\n   */\n  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {\n    if (!templates[name]) {\n      console.warn(`Template \"${name}\" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)\n      return\n    }\n    activeTemplate.value = name\n    try {\n      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)\n    }\n    catch {\n      // Ignore storage errors\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */\n  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(\n    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,\n  )\n\n  /** Metadata for the currently active template */\n  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(\n    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,\n  )\n\n  /** Names of all registered templates */\n  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {\n    return Object.keys(templates)\n  }\n\n  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */\n  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {\n    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)\n  }\n\n  return {\n    activeTemplate,\n    setActiveTemplate,\n    currentTemplate,\n    currentTemplateMetadata,\n    getAvailableTemplates,\n    getAllTemplateMetadata,\n  }\n}\n"
}

     2→  <div class="preview-panel">

     4→    <UAlert

     6→      color="red"
     7→      variant="solid"
     8→      title="XML Parsing Error"
     9→      :description="error"
    10→      icon="i-heroicons-exclamation-triangle"
    11→      class="error-alert"
    12→    />
    13→
    14→    <!-- Loading State -->
    15→    <div v-else-if="isLoading" class="loading-state">
    16→      <p>Parsing XML...</p>
    17→    </div>
    18→
    19→    <!-- Preview Rendering with Zoom Transform -->
    20→    <div
    21→      v-else-if="parsedData && templateComponent"
    22→      class="preview-container"
    23→      :style="containerStyle"
    24→    >
    25→      <component :is="templateComponent" :data="parsedData" />
    26→    </div>
    27→
    28→    <!-- Placeholder State (no data) -->
    29→    <div v-else class="placeholder-state">
    30→      <p>No content to preview. Please provide valid XML.</p>
    31→    </div>
    32→  </div>
    33→</template>
    34→
    35→<script setup lang="ts">
    36→import { ref, computed, watch } from 'vue'
    37→import { useXmlParser } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
    38→import { useTemplate } from '~/composables/useTemplate'
    39→import type { ParsedData } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
    40→
    41→// Ensure this component only runs on the client side (DOMParser is browser-only)
    42→defineOptions({
    43→  name: 'PreviewPanel',
    44→})
    45→
    46→/**
    47→ * PreviewPanel Component
    48→ *
    49→ * Integration point combining XML parser (MVP 2) and template system (MVP 3).
    50→ * Provides real-time preview of XML content with error handling and zoom support.
    51→ *
    52→ * Props:
    53→ * - xmlContent: XML string to parse and render
    54→ * - zoom: Zoom level for scaling (default: 1, range: 0.75 - 1.5)
    55→ */
    56→
    57→interface Props {
    58→  xmlContent: string
    59→  zoom?: number
    60→}
    61→
    62→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
    63→  zoom: 1,
    64→})
    65→
    66→// Reactive state
    67→const parsedData = ref<ParsedData | undefined>(undefined)
    68→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    69→const isLoading = ref(false)
    70→
    71→// Get composables
    72→const { parseXml } = useXmlParser()
    73→const { currentTemplate: templateComponent, activeTemplate } = useTemplate()
    74→
    75→// Computed style for zoom transform
    76→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    77→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    78→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    79→}))
    80→
    81→/**
    82→ * Parse XML and update component state
    83→ * Handles all parsing errors gracefully with user-friendly messages
    84→ */
    85→function updatePreview() {
    86→  isLoading.value = true
    87→  error.value = undefined
    88→  parsedData.value = undefined
    89→
    90→  try {
    91→    const result = parseXml(props.xmlContent)
    92→
    93→    if (result.success && result.data) {
    94→      parsedData.value = result.data
    95→      error.value = undefined
    96→    }
    97→    else {
    98→      error.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
    99→      parsedData.value = undefined
   100→    }
   101→  }
   102→  catch (err) {
   103→    const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
   104→    error.value = `Preview error: ${errorMessage}`
   105→    parsedData.value = undefined
   106→  }
   107→  finally {
   108→    isLoading.value = false
   109→  }
   110→}
   111→
   112→// Re-parse when xmlContent changes, and re-render when active template changes
   113→watch(
   114→  [() => props.xmlContent, activeTemplate],
   115→  () => {
   116→    updatePreview()
   117→  },
   118→  { immediate: true },
   119→)
   120→</script>
   121→
   122→<style scoped>

Let me check if there's a TypeScript issue with assigning a `ComputedRef<Component | undefined>` to `templateComponent` - since we destructure it as `templateComponent`, it will be a `ComputedRef`, not a `Ref`. Vue's template compiler will auto-unwrap the computed ref in both the conditional check and the `:is` binding, so this should work without any issues. ASSISTANTMESSAGE #118
--- ## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`composables/useTemplate.ts`**: Replaced static `ACTIVE_TEMPLATE` constant with reactive `useState('activeTemplate')` shared across components; added `setActiveTemplate()` that persists to `localStorage`; exposed `currentTemplate` as a computed ref; added `onMounted` hook to restore saved template on client mount - **`components/AppHeader.vue`**: Added a `USelectMenu` dropdown labeled "Template:" bound to `activeTemplate` via the composable; selecting an option calls `setActiveTemplate()` immediately - **`components/PreviewPanel.vue`**: Replaced the standalone `getCurrentTemplate()` import with `useTemplate()` composable; `templateComponent` is now the reactive `currentTemplate` computed; the `watch` also tracks `activeTemplate` so template switches trigger instant re-renders ## Key Decisions - Used Nuxt's `useState` (not a module-level `ref`) so state is properly shared across SSR/client boundaries; `onMounted` overrides with the localStorage value after client hydration - Kept `templateComponent` as a `ComputedRef` (from `currentTemplate`) instead of a local `ref`—this means template switches re-render the preview purely through Vue's reactivity, with no imperative calls needed ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feat/template-switcher` - PR: https://github.com/kimwwk/ohmydoc-using-claude-code-agent/pull/22
